target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_scraping" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_scraping</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data scraping</span>"&gt;</span>extraction (<span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>) of data itself<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-han-kamber_6-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Buzzword" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Buzzword</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Buzzword</span>"&gt;</span>buzzword<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-7</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-7" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-7</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;7&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> and is frequently applied to any form of large-scale data or <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value">Information extraction</span>"&gt;</span>extraction<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a any application of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decision_support_system" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Decision_support_system</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Decision support system</span>"&gt;</span>computer decision support system<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, including <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Business_intelligence" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Business_intelligence</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span The book <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>Data mining: Practical machine learning tools and techniques with Java<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-witten-8" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-witten-8</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;8&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> (which covers mostly machine learning material) was originally to be named just <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>Practical machine learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, and the term <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> was only added for marketing reasons.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-9</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> Often the more general terms (<span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>large scale<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>) <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data analysis</span>"&gt;</span>data analysis<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>or, when referring to actual methods, <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>artificial intelligence<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>machine learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>are more appropriate.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="166"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The actual data mining task is the semi-<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/automatic" rel="noreferrer noopener">https://en.wiktionary.org/wiki/automatic</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">extiw</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">wikt:automatic</span>"&gt;</span>automatic<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> or automatic analysis of large quantities of data to extract previously unknown, interesting patterns such as groups of data records (<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cluster_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Cluster_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Cluster analysis</span>"&gt;</span>cluster analysis<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>), unusual records (<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anomaly_detection" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Anomaly_detection</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Anomaly detection</span>"&gt;</span>anomaly detection<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>), and dependencies (<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Association_rule_mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Association_rule_mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Association rule mining</span>"&gt;</span>association rule mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Sequential_pattern_mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Sequential_pattern_mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Sequential pattern mining</span>"&gt;</span>sequential pattern mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>). This usually involves using database techniques such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Spatial_index" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Spatial_index</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Spatial index</span>"&gt;</span>spatial indices<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. These patterns can then be seen as a kind of summary of the input data, and may be used in further analysis or, for example, in machine learning and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Predictive_analytics" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Predictive_analytics</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Predictive analytics</span>"&gt;</span>predictive analytics<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. For example, the data mining step might identify multiple groups in the data, which can then be used to obtain more accurate prediction results by a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decision_support_system" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Decision_support_system</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Decision support system</span>"&gt;</span>decision support system<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. Neither the data collection, data preparation, nor result interpretation and reporting is part of the data mining step, but do belong to the overall KDD process as additional steps.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="167"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The difference between <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data analysis</span>"&gt;</span>data analysis<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and data mining is that data analysis is used to test models and hypotheses on the dataset, e.g., analyzing the effectiveness of a marketing campaign, regardless of the amount of data; in contrast, data mining uses machine learning and statistical models to uncover clandestine or hidden patterns in a large volume of data.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-10</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-10" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-10</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;10&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="168"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The related terms <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_dredging" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_dredging</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data dredging</span>"&gt;</span>data dredging<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data fishing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, and <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data snooping<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> refer to the use of data mining methods to sample parts of a larger population data set that are (or may be) too small for reliable statistical inferences to be made about the validity of any patterns discovered. These methods can, however, be used in creating new hypotheses to test against the larger data populations.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="169"></td><td class="line-content"><span value="208"></td><td class="line-content"><br></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="209"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Etymology</span>"&gt;</span>Etymology<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;action=edit&amp;section=1" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=1</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Etymology</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="210"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>In the 1960s, statisticians and economists used terms like <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data fishing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> or <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data dredging<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> to refer to what they considered the bad practice of analyzing data without an a-priori hypothesis. The term "data mining" was used in a similarly critical way by economist <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Michael_Lovell" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Michael_Lovell</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Michael Lovell</span>"&gt;</span>Michael Lovell<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> in an article published in the <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Review_of_Economic_Studies" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Review_of_Economic_Studies</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Review of Economic Studies</span>"&gt;</span>Review of Economic Studies<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> in 1983.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-11</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-11" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-11</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;11&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-12</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-12" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-12</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;12&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> Lovell indicates that the practice "masquerades under a variety of aliases, ranging from "experimentation" (positive) to "fishing" or "snooping" (negative).</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="211"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The term <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> appeared around 1990 in the database community, generally with positive connotations. For a short time in 1980s, a phrase "database mining", was used, but since it was trademarked by HNC, a San Diego-based company, to pitch their Database Mining Workstation;<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-Mena_13-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-Mena-13" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-Mena-13</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;13&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> researchers consequently turned to <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>. Other terms used include <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data archaeology<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>information harvesting<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>information discovery<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>knowledge extraction<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, etc. <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Gregory_I._Piatetsky-Shapiro" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Gregory_I._Piatetsky-Shapiro</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Gregory I. Piatetsky-Shapiro</span>"&gt;</span>Gregory Piatetsky-Shapiro<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> coined the term "knowledge discovery in databases" for the first workshop on the same topic <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">rel</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">nofollow</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">external text</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="http://www.kdnuggets.com/meetings/kdd89/" rel="noreferrer noopener">http://www.kdnuggets.com/meetings/kdd89/</a>"&gt;</span>(KDD-1989)<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and this term became more popular in <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Artificial_intelligence" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Artificial_intelligence</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Artificial intelligence</span>"&gt;</span>AI<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_learning" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Machine_learning</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Machine learning</span>"&gt;</span>machine learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> community. However, the term data mining became more popular in the business and press communities.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-14</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-14" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-14</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;14&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> Currently, the terms <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>data mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>knowledge discovery<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> are used interchangeably.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="212"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>In the academic community, the major forums for research started in 1995 when the First International Conference on Data Mining and Knowledge Discovery (<span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=KDD-95&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=KDD-95&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;redlink=1</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">new</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">KDD-95 (page does not exist)</span>"&gt;</span>KDD-95<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>) was started in Montreal under <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/AAAI" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/AAAI</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">AAAI</span>"&gt;</span>AAAI<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> sponsorship. It was co-chaired by <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Usama_Fayyad" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Usama_Fayyad</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Usama Fayyad</span>"&gt;</span>Usama Fayyad<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and Ramasamy Uthurusamy. A year later, in 1996, Usama Fayyad launched the journal by Kluwer called <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_Mining_and_Knowledge_Discovery" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_Mining_and_Knowledge_Discovery</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data Mining and Knowledge Discovery</span>"&gt;</span>Data Mining and Knowledge Discovery<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> as its founding editor-in-chief. Later he started the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SIGKDD" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/SIGKDD</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">SIGKDD</span>"&gt;</span>SIGKDD<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> Newsletter SIGKDD Explorations.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-SIGKDD-explorations_15-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-SIGKDD-explorations-15" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-SIGKDD-explorations-15</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;15&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> The KDD International conference became the primary highest quality conference in data mining with an acceptance rate of research paper submissions below 18%. The journal <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>Data Mining and Knowledge Discovery<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> is the primary research journal of the field.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="213"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="214"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Background</span>"&gt;</span>Background<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a Background</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="215"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The manual extraction of patterns from <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data</span>"&gt;</span>data<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> has occurred for centuries. Early methods of identifying patterns in data include <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Bayes%27_theorem" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Bayes%27_theorem</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Bayes&amp;#39; theorem</span>"&gt;</span>Bayes' theorem<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1700s) and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regression_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Regression_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Regression analysis</span>"&gt;</span>regression analysis<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1800s).<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-16</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-16" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-16</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;16&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> The proliferation, ubiquity and increasing power of computer technology have dramatically increased data collection, storage, and manipulation ability. As <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_set" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_set</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data set</span>"&gt;</span>data sets<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> have grown in size and complexity, direct "hands-on" data analysis has increasingly been augmented with indirect, automated data processing, aided by other discoveries in computer science, specially in the field of machine learning, such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Neural_networks" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Neural_networks</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Neural networks</span>"&gt;</span>neural networks<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cluster_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Cluster_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Cluster analysis</span>"&gt;</span>cluster analysis<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Genetic_algorithms" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Genetic_algorithms</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Genetic algorithms</span>"&gt;</span>genetic algorithms<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1950s), <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decision_tree_learning" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Decision_tree_learning</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Decision tree learning</span>"&gt;</span>decision trees<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Decision_rules" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Decision_rules</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Decision rules</span>"&gt;</span>decision rules<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1960s), and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Support_vector_machines" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Support_vector_machines</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Support vector machines</span>"&gt;</span>support vector machines<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (1990s). Data mining is the process of applying these methods with the intention of uncovering hidden patterns.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-Kantardzic_17-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-Kantardzic-17" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-Kantardzic-17</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;17&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> in large data sets. It bridges the gap from <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Applied_statistics" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Applied_statistics</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Applied statistics</span>"&gt;</span>applied statistics<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and artificial intelligence (which usually provide the mathematical background) to <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Database_management" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Database_management</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Database management</span>"&gt;</span>database management<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> by exploiting the way data is stored and indexed in databases to execute the actual learning and discovery algorithms more efficiently, allowing such methods to be applied to ever-larger data sets.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="216"></td><td class="line-content"><span value="233"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>or a simplified process such as (1) Pre-processing, (2) Data Mining, and (3) Results Validation.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="234"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Polls conducted in 2002, 2004, 2007 and 2014 show that the CRISP-DM methodology is the leading methodology used by data miners.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-18</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-18" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-18</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;18&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> The only other data mining standard named in these polls was <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/SEMMA" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/SEMMA</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">SEMMA</span>"&gt;</span>SEMMA<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. However, 34 times as many people reported using CRISP-DM. Several teams of researchers have published reviews of data mining process models,<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-kurgan_19-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-kurgan-19" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-kurgan-19</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;19&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> and Azevedo and Santos conducted a comparison of CRISP-DM and SEMMA in 2008.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-AzevedoSantos_20-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-AzevedoSantos-20" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-AzevedoSantos-20</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;20&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="235"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="236"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Pre-processing</span>"&gt;</span>Pre-processing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;action=edit&amp;section=4" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=4</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Pre-processing</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="237"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Before data mining algorithms can be used, a target data set must be assembled. As data mining can only uncover patterns actually present in the data, the target data set must be large enough to contain these patterns while remaining concise enough to be mined within an acceptable time limit. A common source for data is a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mart" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_mart</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data mart</span>"&gt;</span>data mart<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> or <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_warehouse" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Data_warehouse</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data warehouse</span>"&gt;</span>data warehouse<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. Pre-processing is essential to analyze the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Multivariate_statistics" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Multivariate_statistics</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Multivariate statistics</span>"&gt;</span>multivariate<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> data sets before data mining. The target set is then cleaned. Data cleaning removes the observations containing <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Statistical_noise" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Statistical_noise</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Statistical noise</span>"&gt;</span>noise<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and those with <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Missing_data" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Missing_data</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Missing data</span>"&gt;</span>missing data<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="238"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="239"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Data_mining</span>"&gt;</span>Data mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;action=edit&amp;section=5" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=5</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Data mining</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="240"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Data mining involves six common classes of tasks:<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-Fayyad_5-2</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-Fayyad-5" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-Fayyad-5</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;5&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="241"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="242"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;ul&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Anomaly_detection" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Anomaly_detection</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Anomaly detection</span>"&gt;</span>Anomaly detection<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (outlier/change/deviation detection)  The identification of unusual data records, that might be interesting or data errors that require further investigation.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="243"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Association_rule_learning" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Association_rule_learning</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Association rule learning</span>"&gt;</span>Association rule learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (dependency modeling)  Searches for relationships between variables. For example, a supermarket might gather data on customer purchasing habits. Using association rule learning, the supermarket can determine which products are frequently bought together and use this information for marketing purposes. This is sometimes referred to as market basket analysis.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="244"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cluster_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Cluster_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Cluster analysis</span>"&gt;</span>Clustering<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>  is the task of discovering groups and structures in the data that are in some way or another "similar", without using known structures in the data.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="245"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Statistical_classification" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Statistical_classification</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Statistical classification</span>"&gt;</span>Classification<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>  is the task of generalizing known structure to apply to new data. For example, an e-mail program might attempt to classify an e-mail as "legitimate" or as "spam".<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="246"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Regression_analysis" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Regression_analysis</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Regression analysis</span>"&gt;</span>Regression<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>  attempts to find a function that models the data with the least error that is, for estimating the relationships among data or datasets.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="247"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Automatic_summarization" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Automatic_summarization</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Automatic summarization</span>"&gt;</span>Summarization<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>  providing a more compact representation of the data set, including visualization and report generation.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/li&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/ul&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="248"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" class="html-attribute-value">mbox-text-span</span>"&gt;</span>This section <span class="html-tag">&lt;b&gt;</span>is missing information<span class="html-tag">&lt;/b&gt;</span> about non-classification tasks in data mining. It only covers <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_learning" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Machine_learning</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Machine learning</span>"&gt;</span>machine learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.<span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">hide-when-compact</span>"&gt;</span> Please expand the section to include this information. Further details may exist on the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Talk:Data_mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Talk:Data_mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Talk:Data mining</span>"&gt;</span>talk page<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span>  <span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">date-container</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>(<span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">date</span>"&gt;</span>September 2011<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span>)<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/div&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/td&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/tr&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/tbody&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/table&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="250"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Data mining can unintentionally be misused, and can then produce results that appear to be significant; but which do not actually predict future behavior and cannot be <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Reproducibility" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Reproducibility</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Reproducibility</span>"&gt;</span>reproduced<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> on a new sample of data and bear little use. Often this results from investigating too many hypotheses and not performing proper <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Statistical_hypothesis_testing" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Statistical_hypothesis_testing</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Statistical hypothesis testing</span>"&gt;</span>statistical hypothesis testing<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. A simple version of this problem in <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Machine_learning" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Machine_learning</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Machine learning</span>"&gt;</span>machine learning<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> is known as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Overfitting" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Overfitting</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Overfitting</span>"&gt;</span>overfitting<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, but the same problem can arise at different phases of the process and thus a train/test splitwhen applicable at allmay not be sufficient to prevent this from happening.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-hawkins_21-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-hawkins-21" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-hawkins-21</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;21&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="251"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The final step of knowledge discovery from data is to verify that the patterns produced by the data mining algorithms occur in the wider data set. Not all patterns found by data mining algorithms are necessarily valid. It is common for data mining algorithms to find patterns in the training set which are not present in the general data set. This is called <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Overfitting" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Overfitting</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Overfitting</span>"&gt;</span>overfitting<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. To overcome this, the evaluation uses a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Test_set" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Test_set</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Test set</span>"&gt;</span>test set<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> of data on which the data mining algorithm was not trained. The learned patterns are applied to this test set, and the resulting output is compared to the desired output. For example, a data mining algorithm trying to distinguish "spam" from "legitimate" emails would be trained on a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Training_set" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Training_set</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Training set</span>"&gt;</span>training set<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> of sample e-mails. Once trained, the learned patterns would be applied to the test set of e-mails on which it had <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>not<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span> been trained. The accuracy of the patterns can then be measured from how many e-mails they correctly classify. Several statistical methods may be used to evaluate the algorithm, such as <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Receiver_operating_characteristic" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Receiver_operating_characteristic</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Receiver operating characteristic</span>"&gt;</span>ROC curves<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="252"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>If the learned patterns do not meet the desired standards, subsequently it is necessary to re-evaluate and change the pre-processing and data mining steps. If the learned patterns do meet the desired standards, then the final step is to interpret the learned patterns and turn them into knowledge.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="253"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="254"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span Research</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Standards</span>"&gt;</span>Standards<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a Standards</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h2&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="264"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>There have been some efforts to define standards for the data mining process, for example, the 1999 European <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Cross_Industry_Standard_Process_for_Data_Mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Cross_Industry_Standard_Process_for_Data_Mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Cross Industry Standard Process for Data Mining</span>"&gt;</span>Cross Industry Standard Process for Data Mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (CRISP-DM 1.0) and the 2004 <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Java_Data_Mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Java_Data_Mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Java Data Mining</span>"&gt;</span>Java Data Mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> standard (JDM 1.0). Development on successors to these processes (CRISP-DM 2.0 and JDM 2.0) was active in 2006 but has stalled since. JDM 2.0 was withdrawn without reaching a final draft.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="265"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>For exchanging the extracted modelsin particular for use in <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Predictive_analytics" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Predictive_analytics</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Predictive analytics</span>"&gt;</span>predictive analytics<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>the key standard is the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Predictive_Model_Markup_Language" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Predictive_Model_Markup_Language</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Predictive Model Markup Language</span>"&gt;</span>Predictive Model Markup Language<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (PMML), which is an <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/XML" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/XML</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">XML</span>"&gt;</span>XML<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>-based language developed by the Data Mining Group (DMG) and supported as exchange format by many data mining applications. As the name suggests, it only covers prediction models, a particular data mining task of high importance to business applications. However, extensions to cover (for example) <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Subspace_clustering" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Subspace_clustering</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>While the term "data mining" itself may have no ethical implications, it is often associated with the mining of information in relation to peoples' behavior (ethical and otherwise).<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-27</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="274"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The ways in which data mining can be used can in some cases and contexts raise questions regarding <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-28</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> In particular, data mining government or commercial data sets for national security or law enforcement purposes, such as in the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span Awareness<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> Program or in <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-29</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-30</span>" <span class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Data mining requires data preparation which uncovers information or patterns which compromise confidentiality and privacy obligations. A common way for this to occur is through <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Aggregate_function" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Aggregate_function</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Aggregate function</span>"&gt;</span>data aggregation<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. Data aggregation involves combining data together (possibly from various sources) in a way that facilitates analysis (but that also might make identification of private, individual-level data deducible or otherwise apparent).<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-NASCIO_31-0</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-NASCIO-31" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-NASCIO-31</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;31&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> This is not data mining <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>per se<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, but a result of the preparation of data beforeand for the purposes ofthe analysis. The threat to an individual's privacy comes into play when the data, once compiled, cause the data miner, or anyone who has access to the newly compiled data set, to be able to identify specific individuals, especially when the data were originally anonymous.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-32</span>" <span This indiscretion can cause financial,</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="285"></td><td class="line-content">emotional, or bodily harm to the indicated individual.  In one instance of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Situation_in_Europe</span>"&gt;</span>Situation in Europe<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;action=edit&amp;section=11" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;section=11</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edit section: Situation in Europe</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="290"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_Union" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/European_Union</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">European Union</span>"&gt;</span>Europe<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> has rather strong privacy laws, and efforts are underway to further strengthen the rights of the consumers. However, the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/International_Safe_Harbor_Privacy_Principles" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/International_Safe_Harbor_Privacy_Principles</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">International Safe Harbor Privacy Principles</span>"&gt;</span>U.S.E.U. Safe Harbor Principles<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, developed between 1998 and 2000, currently effectively expose European users to privacy exploitation by U.S. companies. As a consequence of <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Edward_Snowden" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Edward_Snowden</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Edward Snowden</span>"&gt;</span>Edward Snowden<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>'s <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Global_surveillance_disclosure" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Global_surveillance_disclosure</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Global surveillance disclosure</span>"&gt;</span>global surveillance disclosure<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, there has been increased discussion to revoke this agreement, as in particular the data will be fully exposed to the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/National_Security_Agency" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/National_Security_Agency</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">National Security Agency</span>"&gt;</span>National Security Agency<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, and attempts to reach an agreement with the United States have failed.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-37</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-37" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-37</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;37&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="291"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>In the United Kingdom in particular there have been cases of corporations using data mining as a way to target certain groups of customers forcing them to pay unfairly high prices. These groups tend to be people of lower socio-economic status who are not savvy to the ways they can be exploited in digital market places.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-38</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-38" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-38</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;38&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="292"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="293"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Situation_in_the_United_States</span>"&gt;</span>Situation in the United States<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a United States</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="294"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>In the United States, privacy concerns have been addressed by the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/US_Congress" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/US_Congress</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">US Congress</span>"&gt;</span>US Congress<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> via the passage of regulatory controls such as the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Health_Insurance_Portability_and_Accountability_Act" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Health_Insurance_Portability_and_Accountability_Act</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act</span>"&gt;</span>Health Insurance Portability and Accountability Act<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (HIPAA). The HIPAA requires individuals to give their "informed consent" regarding information they provide and its intended present and future uses. According to an article in <span class="html-tag">&lt;i&gt;</span>Biotech Business Week<span class="html-tag">&lt;/i&gt;</span>, "'[i]n practice, HIPAA may not offer any greater protection than the longstanding regulations in the research arena,' says the AAHC. More importantly, the rule's goal of protection through informed consent is approach a level of incomprehensibility to average individuals."<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-39</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-39" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-39</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;39&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> This underscores the necessity for data anonymity in data aggregation and mining practices.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="295"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>U.S. information privacy legislation such as HIPAA and the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Family_Educational_Rights_and_Privacy_Act" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Family_Educational_Rights_and_Privacy_Act</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act</span>"&gt;</span>Family Educational Rights and Privacy Act<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (FERPA) applies only to the specific areas that each such law addresses. The use of data mining by the majority of businesses in the U.S. is not controlled by any legislation.</td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="296"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="297"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h2&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span Europe</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span
