class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="299"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>Under <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Copyright_law_of_the_European_Union" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Copyright_law_of_the_European_Union</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Copyright law of the European Union</span>"&gt;</span>European copyright<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Database_Directive" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Database_Directive</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Database Directive</span>"&gt;</span>database laws<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, the mining of in-copyright works (such as by <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Web_mining" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Web_mining</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Web mining</span>"&gt;</span>web mining<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>) without the permission of the copyright owner is not legal. Where a database is pure data in Europe, it may be that there is no copyrightbut database rights may exist so data mining becomes subject to <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Intellectual_property" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Intellectual_property</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Intellectual property</span>"&gt;</span>intellectual property<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> owners' rights that are protected by the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Database_Directive" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Database_Directive</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Database Directive</span>"&gt;</span>Database Directive<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>. On the recommendation of the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Hargreaves_review&amp;action=edit&amp;redlink=1" rel="noreferrer noopener">/w/index.php?title=Hargreaves_review&amp;amp;action=edit&amp;amp;redlink=1</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">new</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Hargreaves review (page does not exist)</span>"&gt;</span>Hargreaves review<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, this led to the UK government to amend its copyright law in 2014 to allow content mining as a <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Limitations_and_exceptions_to_copyright" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Limitations_and_exceptions_to_copyright</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Limitations and exceptions to copyright</span>"&gt;</span>limitation and exception<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-40</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-40" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-40</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;40&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> The UK was the second country in the world to do so after Japan, which introduced an exception in 2009 for data mining. However, due to the restriction of the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Information_Society_Directive" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Information_Society_Directive</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Information Society Directive</span>"&gt;</span>Information Society Directive<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> (2001), the UK exception only allows content mining for non-commercial purposes. UK copyright law also does not allow this provision to be overridden by contractual terms and conditions. </td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="300"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span>The <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/European_Commission" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/European_Commission</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">European Commission</span>"&gt;</span>European Commission<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> facilitated stakeholder discussion on text and data mining in 2013, under the title of Licences for Europe.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-41</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-41" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-41</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;41&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span> The focus on the solution to this legal issue, such as licensing rather than limitations and exceptions, led to representatives of universities, researchers, libraries, civil society groups and <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Open_access" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Open_access</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Open access</span>"&gt;</span>open access<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> publishers to leave the stakeholder dialogue in May 2013.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-42</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-42" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-42</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;42&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="301"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="302"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;h3&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-headline</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Situation_in_the_United_States_2</span>"&gt;</span>Situation in the United States<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>[<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/w/index.php?title=Data_mining&amp;action=edit&amp;section=15" rel="noreferrer United States</span>"&gt;</span>edit<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;span <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-editsection-bracket</span>"&gt;</span>]<span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/span&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/h3&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="303"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;p&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Copyright_law_of_the_United_States" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Copyright_law_of_the_United_States</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Copyright law of the United States</span>"&gt;</span>US copyright law<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, and in particular its provision for <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Fair_use" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Fair_use</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Fair use</span>"&gt;</span>fair use<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span>, upholds the legality of content mining in America, and other fair use countries such as Israel, Taiwan and South Korea. As content mining is transformative, that is it does not supplant the original work, it is viewed as being lawful under fair use. For example, as part of the <span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Google_Book_Search_Settlement_Agreement" rel="noreferrer noopener">/wiki/Google_Book_Search_Settlement_Agreement</a>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">mw-redirect</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">title</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">Google Book Search Settlement Agreement</span>"&gt;</span>Google Book settlement<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span> the presiding judge on the case ruled that Google's digitization project of in-copyright books was lawful, in part because of the transformative uses that the digitization project displayedone being text and data mining.<span class="html-tag">&lt;sup <span class="html-attribute-name">id</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">cite_ref-43</span>" <span class="html-attribute-name">class</span>="<span class="html-attribute-value">reference</span>"&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;a <span class="html-attribute-name">href</span>="<a class="html-attribute-value html-external-link" target="_blank" href="https://en.wikipedia.org/wiki/Data_mining#cite_note-43" rel="noreferrer noopener">#cite_note-43</a>"&gt;</span>&amp;#91;43&amp;#93;<span class="html-tag">&lt;/a&gt;</span><span class="html-tag">&lt;/sup&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number" value="304"></td><td class="line-content"><span class="html-tag">&lt;/p&gt;</span></td></tr><tr><td class="line-number"
